    Armeria (https://github.com/line/armeria/) is an open-source

    and Java 8. Java 8 required to build this http client module.

commit 60d37feead4a652c59f1a8a9bb2499cbf3c98881
Author: Lucas Werkmeister <mail@lucaswerkmeister.de>
Date:   Thu May 17 23:01:50 2018 +0200

    Add MediaWiki API
    
    This API can be used for any MediaWiki installation that has the OAuth
    extension [1] installed. Two default instances are provided for
    convenience: one for wikis hosted by the Wikimedia Foundation (including
    Wikipedia), which is the one most users will be interested in, and one
    for the Wikimedia Foundation’s Beta Cluster, which is more appropriate
    for testing purposes.
    
    The example is copied and slightly adapted from AWeberExample.java.
    
    [1]: https://www.mediawiki.org/wiki/Extension:OAuth

M	README.md
A	scribejava-apis/src/main/java/com/github/scribejava/apis/MediaWikiApi.java
A	scribejava-apis/src/test/java/com/github/scribejava/apis/examples/MediaWikiExample.java

commit a2887ddc0d724c22a3071eb9c44c8c3db6505bb9
Author: Vivin Paliath <vivin.paliath@gmail.com>
Date:   Wed Mar 29 10:50:01 2017 -0700

    issue #753
    
    Makes `addOAuthParams` and `appendSignature` `protected`, so that they can be used from overridden `prepareRequestTokenRequest` methods in subclasses. This makes it possible to deal with the (rare) case where the request-token endpoint in an OAuth 1.0a service accepts additional-parameters; these are supported by request-token endpoints as per the specification.
